8 /*
9  MATSEQBAIJ format - Block compressed row storage. The i[] and j[]
10  arrays start at 0.
11 */
12 
13 /* This header is shared by the SeqSBAIJ matrix */
14 #define SEQBAIJHEADER \
15  PetscInt bs2; /* square of block size */ \
16  PetscInt mbs,nbs; /* rows/bs, columns/bs */ \
17  PetscScalar *mult_work; /* work array for matrix vector product*/ \
18  PetscScalar *sor_workt; /* work array for SOR */ \
19  PetscScalar *sor_work; /* work array for SOR */ \
20  MatScalar *saved_values; \
21  \
22  Mat sbaijMat; /* mat in sbaij format */ \
23  \
24  \
25  MatScalar *idiag; /* inverse of block diagonal */ \
26  PetscBool idiagvalid /* if above has correct/current values */
27

256 /*
257  PetscKernel_A_gets_A_times_B_2: A = A * B with size bs=2
258 
259  Input Parameters:
260 + A,B - square bs by bs arrays stored in column major order
261 - W - bs*bs work arrary
262 
263  Output Parameter:
264 . A = A * B
265 */
266 
267 #define PetscKernel_A_gets_A_times_B_2(A,B,W) 0; \
268  { \
269  PetscMemcpy(W,A,4*sizeof(MatScalar)); \
270  A[0] = W[0]*B[0] + W[2]*B[1]; \
271  A[1] = W[1]*B[0] + W[3]*B[1]; \
272  A[2] = W[0]*B[2] + W[2]*B[3]; \
273  A[3] = W[1]*B[2] + W[3]*B[3]; \
274  }
275 
276 /*
277  PetscKernel_A_gets_A_minus_B_times_C_2: A = A - B * C with size bs=2
278 
279  Input Parameters:
280 + A,B,C - square bs by bs arrays stored in column major order
281 
282  Output Parameter:
283 . A = A - B*C
284 */
285 
286 #define PetscKernel_A_gets_A_minus_B_times_C_2(A,B,C) 0; \
287  { \
288  A[0] -= B[0]*C[0] + B[2]*C[1]; \
289  A[1] -= B[1]*C[0] + B[3]*C[1]; \
290  A[2] -= B[0]*C[2] + B[2]*C[3]; \
291  A[3] -= B[1]*C[2] + B[3]*C[3]; \
292  }
293 
294 /*
295  PetscKernel_A_gets_A_times_B_3: A = A * B with size bs=3
296 
297  Input Parameters:
298 + A,B - square bs by bs arrays stored in column major order
299 - W - bs*bs work arrary
300 
301  Output Parameter:
302 . A = A * B
303 */
304 
305 #define PetscKernel_A_gets_A_times_B_3(A,B,W) 0; \
306  { \
307  PetscMemcpy(W,A,9*sizeof(MatScalar)); \
308  A[0] = W[0]*B[0] + W[3]*B[1] + W[6]*B[2]; \
309  A[1] = W[1]*B[0] + W[4]*B[1] + W[7]*B[2]; \
310  A[2] = W[2]*B[0] + W[5]*B[1] + W[8]*B[2]; \
311  A[3] = W[0]*B[3] + W[3]*B[4] + W[6]*B[5]; \
312  A[4] = W[1]*B[3] + W[4]*B[4] + W[7]*B[5]; \
313  A[5] = W[2]*B[3] + W[5]*B[4] + W[8]*B[5]; \
314  A[6] = W[0]*B[6] + W[3]*B[7] + W[6]*B[8]; \
315  A[7] = W[1]*B[6] + W[4]*B[7] + W[7]*B[8]; \
316  A[8] = W[2]*B[6] + W[5]*B[7] + W[8]*B[8]; \
317  }
318 
319 /*
320  PetscKernel_A_gets_A_minus_B_times_C_3: A = A - B * C with size bs=3
321 
322  Input Parameters:
323 + A,B,C - square bs by bs arrays stored in column major order
324 
325  Output Parameter:
326 . A = A - B*C
327 */
328 
329 #define PetscKernel_A_gets_A_minus_B_times_C_3(A,B,C) 0; \
